2. Click "Add Candidate" to enter student information.
3. Enter the student's name, grade, historical awards, and click "Confirm".
4. Repeat the above steps for each student you need to add.
5. If you need to modify or delete student information, click "Edit" or "Delete" next to the candidate information.
